( # # # ) appellate court reviews decision trial court point shall:(A ) identify trial court ruling action appellant challenges;(B ) state # # # legal reasons appellant claim reversible error ; and(C ) explain summary fashion context case legal reasons support claim reversible # # # point shall substantially following form : " trial court erred [ identify challenged ruling action ] [ state legal reasons claim reversible error ] [ explain legal reasons context case support claim reversible error ] . " ( # # # ) appellate court reviews decision administrative agency trial court point shall:(A ) identify administrative ruling action appellant challenges;(B ) state # # # legal reasons appellant claim reversible error ; and(C ) explain summary fashion context case legal reasons support claim reversible # # # point shall substantially following form : " [ agency ] erred [ identify challenged ruling action ] [ state legal reasons claim reversible error including reference applicable statute authorizing review ] [ explain context case legal reasons support claim reversible error ] . " ( # # # ) original writ proceeding point shall:(A ) state relief petitioner # # # seeks appellate court;(B ) identify action petitioner # # # challenges;(C ) state # # # legal reasons challenge respondent action ; and(D ) explain summary fashion context case legal reasons support # # # action prohibition point shall substantially following form : " # # # entitled order prohibiting Respondent [ describe challenged action ] [ state legal reasons challenge ] [ explain context case legal reasons support challenge ] .
